# M10 Units #11–14 — sin-NOUN family (shared-substrate family file)

- **File:** wa-m10-units-11to14-sin-noun-family-v1-20260623.md · **v1 · 2026-06-23 · Author:** Claude Code.
- **Units (source: sin-core):** #11 Sin as universal condition · #12 Sin as enslaving power · #13 Sin as divine record · #14 Forgiveness sought and received. (These are the **noun-mode / status faces** of sin — what sin *is* as a standing of the inner person: a universal condition, a mastering power, an accountable record, and the movement toward + receipt of its removal.)
- **Substrate (the NOUNS):** hamartia (G0266) · hamartēma (G0265) · paraptōma (G3900) · chat.tat (H2403B "sin" / H2403H "sin offering" / H2403I) · chet (H2399) · cha.ta.ah (H2401) · chat.ta.ah (H2403A) · al.vah (H5932) · rish.ah (H7564) · kip.pu.rim (H3725 "atonement"). 440 verses in the per-verse section. **The verbs (cha.ta H2398, hamartanō G0264) live in the ḥāṭāʾ sin-act family file — cross-referenced, NOT duplicated here.**
- **What this file is:** the self-contained evidence home for the four noun-mode units — **(A)** general observations on the whole sin-as-noun field + flags, then the four unit sub-sections (collated from the source digests HA / HM / R4 / R2p — *nothing of note left behind*), and **(B)** the per-verse structured substrate (once; shared across the four units; the generator emits full lexical for every term, self-standing). Flag markers per the index method. Evidence only; **highlight, do not resolve.**
- **Index:** `wa-m10-unit-index-1to32-v1-20260623.md`. **Companion:** `wa-m10-units-01to07-15-hatat-sinact-family-v1-20260623.md` (the act-mode verbs — its scope-note flagged the NOUNS as belonging here; this file now migrates the **noun faces** of HA / HM / R4 / R2p). HA / HM / R4 / R2p are **now migrated for the noun faces** and become provenance-only for #11–14.

---

## A. General observations (whole sin-as-noun field)

**Mechanical signature — the Hebrew ḥāṭāʾ nouns (HA digest §1).** Across the ḥāṭāʾ group the **nouns read `status`** (the standing wrong): chet H2399 (33), chat.tat H2403B "sin" (159–160 of 160), cha.ta.ah H2401 (8), chat.ta.ah H2403A (2). All carry **faculty `(none)`** — the status-nouns are NOT faculty-tagged; the inner-being engagement reads from co-terms/co-seated, never from the term. Valence: the "sin" nouns are `sinful`; the **chat.tat sin-offering sub-entry H2403H (110 occ)** is overwhelmingly `neutral 57 / commanded 31 / (none) 7 / sinful 14 / righteous 1` — the cultic remedy, NOT sinful-valence. Book bulk Lev/Num (the cultic sin-offering corpus) + Eze/Psa/Isa/Jer (the moral/record register).

**Mechanical signature — the NT hamart- nouns (HM digest §1).** hamartia (G0266, 105) + hamartēma (G0265, 4) read `status` (the absolute noun "sin"); paraptōma (G3900, R2p) reads `status` "trespass". **Faculty `volition` on ALL hamart- occ (191 family-wide)** — a sharp **cross-language contrast** with the faculty-none Hebrew nouns (see ⚑ SYNTH below). hamartia object_type `none` on 154 (the absolute personified noun — "sin reigns/dwells/enslaves"). Rom dominant (48). Valence `sinful` 183.

**Mechanical signature — kip.pu.rim (H3725, R4 digest).** "Atonement", 8 occ, all the masc-plural noun *kippurim* (a provision/state, not an act — the *acting* is the partner verb ka.phar "to cover"). Valence cultic, never sinful — commanded 2 / neutral 3 / righteous 2. object/object_type 0/8 (extract gap — every verse names what atonement is *for*: altar, lives, him; recoverable from text). Pairs with chat.tat "sin offering" (×3) and cha.ta (×1).

- **⚠ HYGIENE — the chat.tat DOUBLE SENSE (sin AND sin offering).** The single most important diversity in the group: the same lemma names both the offense (chat.tat **H2403B** = "sin", 160 occ, all `status`, all `sinful`; sense sin 88 / sins 67) **and** its cultic remedy (chat.tat **H2403H** = "sin offering", 110 occ, sense "sin offering" 102 + "sin offerings" 4; valence neutral 57 / commanded 31 / (none) 7 / sinful 14 / righteous 1). Any consumer that collapses H2403B + H2403H mis-reads the offering occ as sinful. **Keep the sub-entries distinct.** The **sin face → #11/#13; the sin-OFFERING face → #14 (Forgiveness)** + exploration Thread 1 (atonement). Num 15:27 carries BOTH in one verse (cha.ta "to sin" + chat.tat "sin offering"). **Surface, not resolved.**
- **⚑ SYNTH — the ATONEMENT SEAM (central to this file; exploration Thread 1).** The remedy face of the sin-word is built into the sin-NOUN substrate itself: **chat.tat sin-offering (H2403H, 102+4) + kip.pu.rim (H3725, 8) + Lev 16:30 "atonement… cleanse you… clean from all your sins"** are the *removing-side* apparatus. In the NT this is the forgiveness/borne/cleansing corpus on hamartia/hamartēma (the paralytic-forgiveness cluster; "forgiveness of sins" formula; Joh 1:29 "takes away the sin of the world"; 1Cor 15:3 "Christ died for our sins"; Rom 3:25 propitiation; 2Cor 5:21 "made him to be sin"; Heb sacrifice register; 1Jo confess/cleanse). **The atonement seam is the spine of #14 and reaches back into #13 (the recorded debt that atonement settles).** Surface prominently for the atonement synthesis (see also defilement #29–32 §A — cleansing/purification is the same apparatus).
- **⚑ SYNTH — the faculty=volition cross-language seam (the §10 test case).** The NT hamart- nouns are uniformly tagged `volition` while the Hebrew sin-nouns read `faculty (none)`. Held open: is this a real linguistic fact (the Greek sin-words genuinely encode an act-of-the-will — sin as a *characteristic of the will*) or a uniform family tagging convention masking the same status/verdict character the Hebrew nouns read as faculty-none? Bears directly on whether sin (as a noun/status) is ontologically a *status* or a *faculty-engaged characteristic*. Acute for #12 (enslaving power — the will captive). **Surface, not resolved.**
- **⚑ SYNTH — sin-as-personified-power vs sin-as-condition vs sin-as-record (one noun, three faces).** The single noun **hamartia** carries the **power/dominion** register (Romans 5–8: sin reigns, dwells, enslaves → #12), the **universal-condition** register (Rom 3:23 "all have sinned and fall short" → #11), and the **divine-record/tally** register (Rom 4:8 "not count his sin"; 1Th 2:16 "fill up the measure"; 1Ti 5:24 → #13). Held open whether these are the same object or distinct phenomena the one noun carries; the Pauline register personifies, the Gospel/Johannine often does not. **Surface, not resolved.** (Per-occurrence which-face assignment → §10, except the clear anchors named per unit.)
- **⚑ SYNTH — sin as a borne / recorded / removable STANDING (the divine-record register).** chet (H2399) and cha.ta.ah (H2401) behave as an object that is pardoned / cleansed / written / blotted out: **Jer 17:1 ("The sin of Judah is written with a pen of iron… engraved on the tablet of their heart"); Isa 40:2 ("her sins… double from the Lord's hand" — the reckoned account); Isa 43:25 ("I… blot out your transgressions… and I will not remember your sins"); Lev 16:30 ("clean… from all your sins").** This recorded/accumulated/named/blotted-out behaviour is the substance of #13 and interlocks with #14 (what is recorded is what atonement blots out). **Surface.**
- **⚠ HYGIENE — al.vah (H5932) and rish.ah (H7564) are thin/marginal here.** al.vah ("injustice/the unjust") carries an empty gloss in places — **resolved by reading** to "the unjust" (Hos 10:9, touching cha.ta; R2p §1). rish.ah ("wickedness") sits primarily in the wickedness family (M10b ra'sha cluster) — included for the #11 universal-condition net but its characteristic-home is the wickedness units, not the sin-noun units. **Flag the borrow; do not over-weight.**
- **⚠ HYGIENE — faculty is term-intrinsic; object vs object_type.** The hamart- `volition` and any moral_evaluation tags are properties of the head term, NOT verse-level inner-faculty readings — verse interior reads from co-terms/co-seated. Trust object_type over object text (e.g. Rom 6:11 object="dead"; Rom 5:8 object=""; Gal 2:17 object="Christ" type=abstract). object_type=`none` on the absolute-noun usages is correct silence, not a gap.
- **⚠ HYGIENE — bounded interior; the ne.phesh idiom.** The genuine inner signal is sparse. Hebrew nouns: the heart-seatings are few (Jer 17:1 sin "engraved on the tablet of their **heart**"; Isa 40:2 sins // tablet). The **ne.phesh co-seatings are mostly the "life/soul" idiom** ("sin against innocent blood/life"), NOT soul-seating — genuine resonance only Eze 18:20 ("the **soul** who sins shall die"); Mic 6:7; Hos 4:8. NT (richer, Romans-weighted): the constitutional seats on hamartia — **flesh (sarx) Rom 7:5,25; 8:3 · mind (nous) Rom 7:23,25 · spirit (pneuma) Rom 8:2,10 · heart (kardia) Rom 6:17 "obedient from the heart" · conscience (suneidesis) 1Cor 8:12 · soul (psuchē) Heb 12:3; Jam 5:20** — the explicit Pauline anthropology of sin's dwelling-place (13 of 191 co-seated; do not over-read but DO note it is qualitatively richer than the Hebrew status-nouns' bounded seats). **These feed any M47 (Constitution) cross-reference.**

**↔ BOND (cross-cluster, for §A — these noun-mode units bond dominantly with):**
- **↔ BOND — M11 (Repentance / Forgiveness) — DOMINANT, esp. #14 (83 shared verses).** The being-forgiven counterpart; afiēmi the standing partner of the forgiveness-of-sins corpus; shuv "turn"; the confess/cleanse seam (1Jo). The #14 home-bond.
- **↔ BOND — M38 (Salvation) — #14 (51 shared verses).** The borne-for / died-for-our-sins / "to save sinners" register (Joh 1:29; 1Cor 15:3; 1Ti 1:15) that answers the recorded debt.
- **↔ BOND — M26 (Righteousness).** The structural antithesis framing the whole field — sinner-vs-righteous; "set free from sin… become slaves of righteousness" (Rom 6); the record reckoned against righteousness.
- **↔ BOND — M12 (Purity).** The cleanse/purify remedy register (Lev 16:30; Psa 51:2; Act 22:16 "washed away"); the atonement-seam bond — purification is the same apparatus (cf. defilement #29–32).
- **↔ BOND — M47 (Constitution / seats).** The heart/flesh/mind/spirit/conscience seats sin dwells in / is recorded on (the bounded-interior evidence above feeds the M47 cross-reference).
- **↔ BOND — M23 (Strength / dominion).** For #12 specifically — the kurieuō "lord over" / basileuō "reign" / dunamis "power" / douleuō "enslave" partner web (Rom 6; 1Cor 15:56 "the power of sin").

**⚖ BORDER — shared-substrate / per-occurrence assignment (governing for this file).** Units **#11 / #12 / #13 / #14 share hamartia and chat.tat**. Per-occurrence assignment (which hamartia is power vs record vs condition; which chat.tat is sin vs offering) is **DEFERRED to §10 except where the reading is CLEAR**: Romans dominion (reigns/dwells/enslaves) → **#12**; "all have sinned / fall short / under sin" → **#11**; blot-out / written / measure / count → **#13**; sin-OFFERING / atonement / forgiveness-of-sins / borne-for → **#14**. Overlap across units is expected and washes out in analysis.

**⚖ BORDER — is "sin offering" a face of sin at all? (the central §10 status-vs-characteristic test).** The ḥāṭāʾ group forces the question for the whole cluster: chat.tat carries both the sin (H2403B) and the sin-offering (H2403H) in one lemma. If M10 "Sin" is the *status/characteristic* of being-in-sin, the **sin-offering (H2403H, 110 occ, neutral/commanded valence, Lev/Num cultic)** may not belong to the sin-status units at all — it is the *removal* of the status, properly #14 (the remedy). Recorded as the central status-vs-characteristic test for M10: is "sin offering" a face of sin, or of its undoing? **Held open (assigned to #14 here as the remedy, flagged for §10).**

---

### Unit #11 — Sin as universal condition
- **DEF (DB):** the structural condition of the inner person — fall-short-of-glory; the state under which every person stands; sin as the universal human standing, not a single act (Rom 3:23 "all have sinned").
- **Terms/salient:** hamartia (G0266), hamartēma (G0265), paraptōma (G3900), chat.tat (H2403B), al.vah (H5932), rish.ah (H7564).
- **Observations (HM §2e — PRIMARY; HA §2b2; R2p).** The NT universal-condition register: **Rom 3:23 ("all have sinned and fall short of the glory of God") — the NT anchor**; Rom 3:9 ("all… are under sin"); Gal 3:22 ("imprisoned everything under sin"); Rom 5:12 ("sin came into the world… death spread to all because all sinned"); Rom 3:20; 7:7 ("knowledge of sin" through the law); Joh 9:34 ("born in utter sin"); Joh 8:21,24 ("die in your sin(s)"). Hebrew innate register: Psa 51:5 ("in sin did my mother conceive me" — HA §2b2). al.vah/rish.ah net in the universal-standing register (the unjust/wicked condition). paraptōma "dead in trespasses" (Eph 2:1,5) is the corporate fallen-standing.
- **Signature:** the absolute-noun hamartia with object_type=none; the "under sin" / "all sinned" frame.
- **Salient (clear reading):** Rom 3:23; Rom 3:9; Rom 5:12; Gal 3:22; Joh 8:21; Joh 8:24; Psa 51:5; Eph 2:1.
- **⚖ BORDER:** shares hamartia with #12/#13 — distinguished by the "all/under" universal reading; beyond the clear anchors, assignment deferred to §10.
- **⚑ SYNTH:** the universal condition is the *standing* sin produces in everyone — interlocks with #12 (the power that holds the condition in place) and #14 (the remedy that lifts it). The faculty=volition seam (§A) bears on whether the condition is a will-state or a status. **Surface.**

### Unit #12 — Sin as enslaving power
- **DEF (DB):** active force / power mastering the inner person — the will captive under sin's dominion (Romans 5–8: sin reigns / dwells / enslaves).
- **Terms/salient:** hamartia (G0266). *(The act-verb hamartanō G0264 — "practices sin is a slave to sin", Joh 8:34 — lives in the sin-ACT family file; cross-referenced.)*
- **Observations (HM §2a — PRIMARY, the strongest single behaviour of the noun, concentrated in Romans).** Sin is an **agent/sovereign**: it "came into the world" and **"reigned"** (Rom 5:12,21), "increased" (5:20), told **not to "reign in your mortal body"** (Rom 6:12), has/has-no **"dominion"** (Rom 6:14, *kurieuō* "lord over"); persons are **"slaves of sin / enslaved to sin / sold under sin / set free from sin"** (Rom 6:6,16,17,18,20,22; 7:14, with *douleuō/doulos/douloō* M36 partners); sin **"dwells within me"** (Rom 7:17,20,23,25), **"seized an opportunity, deceived, killed"** (Rom 7:8,11); the **"law of sin"** wages war (Rom 7:23,25; 8:2). Joh 8:34 ("a slave to sin"). 1Cor 15:56 ("the **power** of sin is the law", *dunamis* partner). This face accounts for most of the 154 object_type=none (sin as absolute personified noun).
- **Signature:** the personified-power register — sin as subject of reign/dwell/enslave verbs; the Pauline constitutional seats (flesh/mind/spirit, Rom 6–8) cluster here.
- **Salient (clear reading):** Rom 5:21; Rom 6:6; Rom 6:12; Rom 6:14; Rom 7:17; Rom 7:23; Joh 8:34; 1Cor 15:56.
- **↔ BOND:** **M23 (Strength/dominion)** — the lord-over/reign/power partner web; **M47 (Constitution)** — the flesh/mind/spirit dwelling-place of the dominion.
- **⚑ SYNTH:** the faculty=volition seam is most acute here — "the will captive" is the DB definition; is the captivity a real will-encoding or a tag? **Surface.** Also held open whether sin-as-power (here) is the same object as sin-as-condition (#11) and sin-as-record (#13), or distinct phenomena the one noun carries.

### Unit #13 — Sin as divine record
- **DEF (DB):** objective moral weight before God — recorded / accumulated / named; blotted out, written (Jer 17:1 "engraved"; Isa 43:25 "blot out").
- **Terms/salient:** the ḥāṭāʾ nouns chat.tat (H2403B/H2403H/H2403I), chet (H2399), cha.ta.ah (H2401), chat.ta.ah (H2403A), hamartēma (G0265), hamartia (G0266).
- **Observations (HA §2d — the LARGEST face; HM §2g).** The status-nouns as a borne / recorded / removable standing: **Jer 17:1 ("The sin of Judah is written with a pen of iron… engraved on the tablet of their heart")**; **Isa 40:2 ("her sins… double from the Lord's hand" — the reckoned account)**; **Isa 43:25 ("I… blot out your transgressions for my own sake, and I will not remember your sins")**; Lev 16:30 ("clean… from all your sins"). NT divine-record/tally (HM §2g): **1Th 2:16 ("fill up the measure of their sins"); 1Ti 5:24 ("the sins of some are conspicuous, going before them to judgment… others appear later"); Rom 4:8 ("the Lord will not count his sin"); Act 7:60 ("do not hold this sin against them").** The "borne / counted" object behaviour — sin as a tally that accumulates and is settled.
- **Signature:** the chet/chat.tat/cha.ta.ah status-nouns as recorded objects; the write/blot-out/measure/count verb-partners; the heart as the tablet sin is engraved on (Jer 17:1 — the one genuine heart-seat in this register).
- **Salient (clear reading):** Jer 17:1; Isa 40:2; Isa 43:25; 1Th 2:16; 1Ti 5:24; Rom 4:8; Act 7:60.
- **⚖ BORDER:** the divine record is the debt that **#14 (atonement) blots out** — #13 (the recorded standing) and #14 (its removal) are the obverse/reverse of the same accounting; verses naming both (Lev 16:30 record→cleanse; Isa 43:25 sins→blot-out) bridge the two. Per-occurrence which-unit deferred to §10.
- **⚑ SYNTH:** the recorded/accumulated register is the objective face of sin (weight before God), distinct from the subjective faces (#11 condition, #12 power) — surface the objective/subjective axis. **Surface.**

### Unit #14 — Forgiveness sought and received
- **DEF (DB):** the inner movement toward God seeking forgiveness + the divine response — the ATONEMENT mechanism (the removing-side of sin).
- **Terms/salient:** chat.tat (H2403H "sin-offering"), kip.pu.rim (H3725), paraptōma (G3900), cha.ta.ah (H2401), hamartia / hamartēma.
- **Observations (HA §2a + face(a); R4 in full; HM §2d; R2p).**
  - **The chat.tat sin-OFFERING (H2403H, 102+4):** the cultic remedy named by the very word for the offense — Exo 29:14,36; 30:10; Lev 4:8,20,21,24,25; **Lev 16:30 ("on this day shall atonement be made for you to cleanse you… clean from all your sins")**; concentration Lev 47 / Num 36 / Exo 3 / Eze 14 / 2Ch 3. Valence cultic (neutral/commanded), NOT sinful. **⚠ HYGIENE: this is the H2403H sub-entry — keep distinct from H2403B "sin".**
  - **kip.pu.rim "atonement" (H3725, 8; R4):** the masc-plural noun = a provision/state; partner verb **ka.phar/kip.per "to cover/atone" (8)** is the constant act; applied to the **altar** (Exo 29:36; 30:10), the **persons/their lives** (Exo 30:16 "for your lives"), individuals (Num 5:8; Lev 23:28). Largely objective/external (blood, atonement money, ram). **One inner-being thread (R4 §3, held open):** on the Day of Atonement the people must **"afflict yourselves / your souls" (nephesh, Lev 23:27)** — the self/soul humbled as part of the atonement day (partner *a.nah* "to afflict"); atonement "for your lives" (Exo 30:16). The remedy touches the inner being (soul afflicted, life ransomed) alongside the dominant external covering. **⚠ HYGIENE: kip.pu.rim object/object_type 0/8 — extract gap; the object of atonement (altar/lives/him) is in the verse text, recoverable.**
  - **The NT forgiveness/borne/cleansing corpus on hamartia/hamartēma (HM §2d):** sin **forgiven** (the paralytic cluster, *afiēmi* M11 partner — Mat 9:2,5,6; Mar 2:5–10; Luk 5:20–24; 7:47–49; Joh 20:23); **"forgiveness of sins"** proclaimed (Mat 26:28; Mar 1:4; Luk 1:77; 24:47; Act 2:38; 5:31; 10:43; 13:38; 26:18; Col 1:14); **blotted out / washed away** (Act 3:19; 22:16); **covered / not counted** (Rom 4:7,8); **borne / died for** ("the Lamb of God who takes away the sin of the world" Joh 1:29; "Christ died for our sins" 1Cor 15:3; "gave himself for our sins" Gal 1:4; "propitiation… passed over former sins" Rom 3:25; "made him to be sin who knew no sin" 2Cor 5:21); purification/sacrifice (Heb 1:3; 2:17; 7:27; 9–10); **confessed** (Mat 3:6; Mar 1:5); 1Jo confess/cleanse ("an advocate with the Father" 1Jo 2:1; 1:9).
  - **paraptōma (R2p):** "trespass" tightly paired with **grace and forgiveness** — the remedy sits right beside it ("not counting their trespasses" 2Cor 5:19; Adam's trespass answered by grace, Rom 5).
- **Signature:** the cultic remedy (chat.tat-offering + kip.pu.rim) + the NT forgiveness corpus; the only sin-noun unit with predominantly non-sinful valence (the remedy face).
- **Salient (clear reading):** Lev 16:30; Exo 30:10; Num 5:8; Lev 23:27 (afflict the soul); Joh 1:29; 1Cor 15:3; Rom 3:25; Act 22:16; 2Cor 5:19; 1Jo 1:9.
- **↔ BOND:** **M11 (Repentance/Forgiveness) DOMINANT (83 shared)** — the being-forgiven home; **M38 (Salvation, 51 shared)** — the borne-for/save-sinners register; **M12 (Purity)** — the cleanse/wash remedy.
- **⚑ SYNTH — ATONEMENT SEAM (central):** #14 is the spine of the atonement seam (§A). The sin-offering = the sin-word naming its own remedy; kip.pu.rim = the covering; the NT corpus = its fulfilment. Reaches back into #13 (the recorded debt atonement blots out). The defilement-cleansing apparatus (#29–32) is the same machinery (purification). **Surface prominently — Thread 1.**
- **⚖ BORDER:** whether the sin-OFFERING belongs to a "sin" characteristic at all, or only to forgiveness/remedy (the central §10 test, §A) — assigned to #14 here as the remedy, flagged for §10.

---

## B. Per-verse structured evidence (shared substrate, once)

The four units above draw their salient verses from this substrate; the generator emits **full lexical for every term** (self-standing). Per-occurrence axis-assignment (which verse → which unit) is **deferred to §10** except where flagged salient above. **⚖ BORDER:** units #11–#14 share the hamartia / chat.tat substrate — verse→unit assignment is by reading, not lemma. **⚠ HYGIENE:** chat.tat appears as both H2403B "sin" (→ #11/#13) and H2403H "sin offering" (→ #14) — read the sub-entry. **The verbs (cha.ta H2398, hamartanō G0264) are NOT in this substrate — see the sin-act family file.**

#### Gen 18:20
> Gen 18:20 Then the Lord said , “Because the outcry against Sodom and Gomorrah is great and their sin is very grave ,
- **chat.tat (H2403B)** — sin  [Hebrew · M10 · **FOCUS**]  morph=HNcfsc · target=“sin”
  - sense=sin · lemma_meaning=sin, sinful thing · type=status · how=great (H7231) · cause=conduct of Sodom and Gomorrah · cause_clause=sin very grave · experiencer=other · intensity=['many (great)', 'very (very)'] · valence=sinful

*Sin-noun family file. General collated from HA / HM / R4 / R2p digests (now migrated for the noun faces; provenance-only). Per-verse full-lexical substrate (all terms) from corpus. The verbs (cha.ta / hamartanō) are in the sin-act family file — not duplicated. No synthesis; flags surfaced; held open pending §10.*
